info:Hot Spring Room - Mountain-View (2 beds)
info:Stayed in May 2024
info:Family
info:2 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted May 9, 2024
msg:Hongzhushan Hotel is located next to Baoguo Temple at the foot of Mount Emei, one of the four major Buddhist holy sites in China. You can hear the morning bells and evening drums, and feel the spiritual energy of the fairy mountain. There are 440,000 square meters of virgin forest, 100,000 square meters of natural lakes surrounding it, and forest radon hot springs with a mineralization age of more than 20 million years with a negative oxygen ion content 3,000 times that of cities, and 5,000 meters of forest hiking trails. The overall layout of the hotel is backed by mountains and faces water, with dispersed correspondence; the individual buildings are based on the mountain, forming a unique downward-extending structure. You can appreciate the unparalleled natural environment in the hotel without leaving the house. Looking down at the whole hotel, 9 villa-style floors are hidden on the side of the peaks, in the valley, and in the corner of the lake. There are pavilions, waterside pavilions, small bridges and guest-only walking paths in between, forming a unique landscape of natural scenery and pavilions. As soon as I arrived at the hotel, I met the housekeeper Xiao Gao. He was very enthusiastic to help us check in and take us to the room. He was very considerate. I experienced copying scriptures and told me about the room facilities and equipment. He also told me about nearby food spots and going up the mountain. The transportation here is convenient, the environment is good, the rooms are clean and tidy, the lobby is very Zen, the hot springs here are very comfortable, and there are local snacks to choose from for breakfast. It is really a hotel for vacation and tourism. Recommended ğŸ‘
